86:["$","span","span-10",{"data-line":"","children":[["$","span","span-0",{"style":{"--shiki-light":"#24292E","--shiki-dark":"#ABB2BF"},"children":"                <"}],["$","span","span-1",{"style":{"--shiki-light":"#22863A","--shiki-dark":"#E06C75"},"children":"ui:Label"}],["$","span","span-2",{"style":{"--shiki-light":"#6F42C1","--shiki-dark":"#D19A66"},"children":"
